<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eghel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*igil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*igilaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁eǵʰis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hedgehog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Echel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leech</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> commonly thought to be related to this term.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*aij</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ajją</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ōwyóm</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">own</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aard.html>aard</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nature, character, disposition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">eigenartig</i>: having a nature of its own.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>idiosyncratic, peculiar</li></ol>

***eigennaam.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigennaam.html>eigennaam</a> (118135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">own, proper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">name</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eigennaam.html>eigennaam</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eigennamen.html>eigennamen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eigennaam.html>eigennaampje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>proper noun, the (capitalized) name of a particular person, place, organization or other individual entity</li></ol>

***eikelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eikelen.html>eikelen</a> (131440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eikel.html>eikel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">acorn, jerk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eikelen.html>eikelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> particularly relating to pigs</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to (let) forage for acorns
<ul><li><b>1990</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:willy.html>Willy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Braekman, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>nieuws</a> in d'hand. Marktliederen, rolzangers <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volkse.html>volkse</a> poëzie <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weleer.html>weleer</a></i>, 53.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> varkenshoeder <a href = vnd.unilang:geprobeerd.html>geprobeerd</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> winter, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eikelen.html>eikelen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zwijnen.html>zwijnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorbij.html>voorbij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afdanken.html>afgedankt</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1997</b>, Chr. Buiks, <i>Laatmiddeleeuws <a href = vnd.unilang:landschap.html>landschap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> veldnamen in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Baronie <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:breda.html>Breda</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Gorcum, 68.
<dl><dd>In <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Mastbos <a href = vnd.unilang:groeiden.html>groeiden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eiken.html>eiken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sprake.html>sprake</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:varkens.html>varkens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> mast <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eikelen.html>eikelden</a></b>.
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> no oaks growing in the Mastbos and there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never any mention of pigs who <b>foraged for acorns</b> from the mast there.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2002</b> March, <a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> Baeté amp; Kris Vandekerkhove, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>Leren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verleden.html>verleden</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> historiek <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> bosreservaat Kersselaerspleyn in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Zoniënwoud</i>, in <i>BosreservatenNieuws</i>, nr. 2, 3.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omvangrijk.html>omvangrijke</a> bedrijvigheid <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewijzen.html>bewijzen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:periode.html>periode</a> : <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> 5900 <a href = vnd.unilang:varkens.html>varkens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mocht.html>mocht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bos.html>bos</a> ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:eikelen.html>eikelen</a></b>’.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2006</b> January, H. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Haaster, <i>Archeobotanisch <a href = vnd.unilang:onderzoek.html>onderzoek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkele.html>enkele</a> grondmonsters <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:periode.html>periode</a> Romeinse Tijd-Vroege <a href = vnd.unilang:middeleeuwen.html>Middeleeuwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:locatie.html>locatie</a> Dommelsvoort <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> Beers (gem. Cuijk)</i>, in Biax<i>iaal</i> 255, Biax Consult, 12.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>Uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaan.html>bestaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regels.html>regels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afleiden.html>afleiden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eikelen.html>eikelen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:varkens.html>varkens</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:bossen.html>bossen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> toegepaste <a href = vnd.unilang:praktijk.html>praktijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> can infer from the existence of these rules that letting pigs <b>forage on acorns</b> in forests <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a common practice.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be annoying, to act like a jerk
<ul><li><b>2011</b>, Joost Heyink, "<a href = vnd.unilang:zwarte.html>Zwarte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engel.html>engel</a>", <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a> Unieboek/<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> Spectrum (publ.).
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>Om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belachelijk.html>belachelijkste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaten.html>zaten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ouders.html>ouders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eikelen.html>eikelen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuten.html>minuten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoenen.html>zoenen</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eiland.html>eiland</a> (1327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eilant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*eilant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:eiland.html>eiland</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*awjōlandą</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">island</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The former part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*awjō</i>, the latter identical to modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i>.
</p>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eilandengroep.html>eilandengroep</a> (83721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eiland.html>eiland</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eisen.html>eisen</a> (2696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eischen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*eiskon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiskōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eisen.html>eisen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to demand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to claim
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ramp.html>ramp</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eiste.html>eiste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 155 <a href = vnd.unilang:personen.html>personen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The disaster <b><a href = vnd.unilang:claimed.html>claimed</a></b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> of 155 individuals.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to require</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">eiaculatio</i>; from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ejaculeren.html>ejaculeren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-atie</i>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">egestre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">exter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*agastra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*agastrijā</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>Eurasian magpie, <i>Pica pica</i>.</li>
<li>A magpie, any bird of the genus <i>Pica</i>.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">elant</i>, from obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:elen.html>elen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">elend</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:elen.html>elen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">elent</i>.

***elasticiteit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:elasticiteit.html>elasticiteit</a> (49622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">élasticité</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐλαστός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">elastós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ductile, flexible</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐλαύνω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">elaúnō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strike, beat out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself of of uncertain origin. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elastisch.html>elastisch</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-iteit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elasticiteit.html>elasticiteit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elasticiteit.html>elasticiteiten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The property elasticity, by virtue of which a material can regain its original dimensions.</li></ol>

***elektrocardiogram.html

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">electro-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cardiogram.html>cardiogram</a></i>, possibly borrowed.
